  <a id="2015" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="2020" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="2023" <a id="2430" class="Comment">{- Definition 18.1.2 The dependent universal property of pushouts -}</a>

  <a id="2541" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2542" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2542" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="2545" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2545" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="2548" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2548" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="2551" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2551" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="2554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2556" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2561" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2564" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2564" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2568" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2573" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2576" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2576" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2580" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2583" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2542" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="2585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2587" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2588" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2588" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2592" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2595" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2545" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="2597" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2599" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2600" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2600" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2602" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2604" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2607" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2548" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="2609" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="2613" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2614" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2614" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2616" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2618" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2576" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2620" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2622" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2588" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2623" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2625" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2626" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2626" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2630" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2576" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2632" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2634" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2600" class="Bound">B</a><a id="2635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2637" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2638" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2638" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="2640" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2642" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2645" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2551" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="2647" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2650" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2650" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="2652" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2654" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.24-pushouts.html#1435" class="Function">cocone</a> <a id="2661" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2614" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2663" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2626" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2665" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2638" class="Bound">X</a><a id="2666" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2668" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2670" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2673" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="2675" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2500" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-pushout</a> <a id="2712" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2712" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2714" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2714" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2716" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2716" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2718" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2719" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2719" class="Bound">X</a><a id="2720" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2722" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2722" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="2724" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="2728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2729" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2729" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="2731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2733" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2719" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="2735" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2737" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2740" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2712" class="Bound">l</a><a id="2741" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2745" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1556" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="2754" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2755" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#1789" class="Function">dep-cocone-map</a> <a id="2770" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2714" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2772" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2716" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2774" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2722" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="2776" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#2729" class="Bound">P</a><a id="2777" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="2780" class="Comment">{- Remark 18.1.3. We compute the identity type of dep-cocone in order to 
   express the computation rules of the induction principle for pushouts. -}</a>

   version of the pullback property of pushouts. -}</a>

<a id="11208" class="Comment">{- Theorem 18.1.4 The following properties are all equivalent:
 
   1. universal-property-pushout
   2. pullback-property-pushout
   3. dependent-pullback-property-pushout
   4. dependent-universal-property-pushout
   5. Ind-pushout

   We have already shown that 1 ↔ 2. Therefore we will first show that 
   3 ↔ 4 ↔ 5. Finally, we will show that 2 ↔ 3. Here are the precise references
   to the proofs of those parts:

   Proof of 1 → 2.
   pullback-property-pushout-universal-property-pushout

   Proof of 2 → 1
   universal-property-pushout-pullback-property-pushout

   Proof of 2 → 3
   dependent-pullback-property-pullback-property-pushout

   Proof of 3 → 2
   pullback-property-dependent-pullback-property-pushout

   Proof of 3 → 4
   dependent-universal-property-dependent-pullback-property-pushout

   Proof of 4 → 3
   dependent-pullback-property-dependent-universal-property-pushout

   Proof of 4 → 5
   Ind-pushout-dependent-universal-property-pushout

   Proof of 5 → 4
   dependent-universal-property-pushout-Ind-pushout
   -}</a>

<a id="12253" class="Comment">{- Proof of Theorem 18.1.4, (v) implies (iv). -}</a>

              <a id="18756" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18758" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18760" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18760" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="18762" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18764" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="18768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18769" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#17370" class="Function">tr-triv</a> <a id="18777" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18778" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18009" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="18780" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18760" class="Bound">s</a><a id="18781" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18783" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18784" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18453" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="18786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18787" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#17999" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18790" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#17989" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18792" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18760" class="Bound">s</a><a id="18793" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="18813" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18815" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18817" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18817" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="18819" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18821" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#9049" class="Function">apd</a> <a id="18825" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18453" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="18827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18828" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18009" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="18830" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18817" class="Bound">s</a><a id="18831" class="Symbol">)))))))</a>
    <a id="18843" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18845" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18013" class="Bound">dpb</a> <a id="18849" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18852" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18852" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18854" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18856" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18017" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="18857" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="18861" class="Comment">{- Proof of Theorem 18.1.4, (ii) implies (iii). -}</a>

<a id="18913" class="Comment">{- We first define the family of lifts, which is indexed by maps Y → X. -}</a>

  <a id="20848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20849" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18989" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="20859" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20775" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20861" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20801" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="20863" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20833" class="Bound">h</a><a id="20864" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20869" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#18989" class="Function">fam-lifts</a> <a id="20879" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20763" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20881" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20801" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="20883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20884" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20833" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="20886" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="20888" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20819" class="Bound">f</a><a id="20889" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="20892" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20719" class="Function">precompose-lifts</a> <a id="20909" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20909" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="20911" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20911" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20913" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20913" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="20915" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20915" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="20918" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20918" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="20920" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20922" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20915" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="20925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20926" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20911" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20928" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-descent.html#20918" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20929" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="20932" class="Comment">{- Given two homotopic maps, their precomposition functions have different 
   codomains. However, there is a commuting triangle. We obtain this triangle
   by homotopy induction. -}</a>

<a id="23282" class="Comment">{- There is a coherence between the two commuting triangles. This coherence
   is again constructed by homotopy induction. -}</a>

<a id="26250" class="Comment">{- Our goal is now to produce a homotopy between (precompose-total-lifts P f) 
   and (precompose-total-lifts P g) for homotopic maps f and g, and a coherence
   filling a cilinder. -}</a>

<a id="38795" class="Comment">{- Theorem 18.2.3 -}</a>

<a id="43685" class="Comment">{-
-- Section 18.3 The Flattening lemma for pushouts

{- Definition 18.3.1 -}

cocone-flattening-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  { S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  ( f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X)
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  cocone
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( Σ X Q)
cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e =
  pair
    ( map-Σ Q
      ( pr1 c)
      ( λ a → map-equiv (pr1 e a)))
    ( pair
      ( map-Σ Q
        ( pr1 (pr2 c))
        ( λ b → map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) b)))
      ( htpy-map-Σ Q
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → map-equiv (pr1 e (f s)))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s))))

{- Theorem 18.3.2 The flattening lemma -}

coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; :
  {l1 l2 l3 : Level} {B : UU l1} {Q : B → UU l2} {T : UU l3}
  {b b&#39; : B} (α : Id b b&#39;) {y : Q b} {y&#39; : Q b&#39;} (β : Id (tr Q α y) y&#39;)
  (h : (b : B) → Q b → T) → Id (h b y) (h b&#39; y&#39;)
coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; refl refl h = refl

coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {P : A → UU l3} {Q : B → UU l4} {T : UU l5}
  {f f&#39; : A → B} (H : f ~ f&#39;)
  {g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)}
  {g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a)}
  (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a))
  (h : (b : B) → Q b → T) → (a : A) (p : P a) →
  Id (h (f a) (g a p)) (h (f&#39; a) (g&#39; a p))
coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H K h a p =
  coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma&#39; (H a) (K a p) h

coherence-cube-flattening-lemma :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {P : A → UU l3} {Q : B → UU l4} {T : UU l5}
  {f f&#39; : A → B} (H : f ~ f&#39;)
  {g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)}
  {g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a)}
  (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a))
  (h : Σ B Q → T) →
  Id ( eq-htpy
       ( λ a → eq-htpy
         ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H K (ev-pair h) a)))
     ( ap ev-pair
       ( htpy-precomp (htpy-map-Σ Q H g K) T h))
coherence-cube-flattening-lemma {A = A} {B} {P} {Q} {T} {f = f} {f&#39;} H {g} {g&#39;} K = ind-htpy f
    ( λ f&#39; H&#39; →
      (g : (a : A) → P a → Q (f a)) (g&#39; : (a : A) → P a → Q (f&#39; a))
      (K : (a : A) → ((tr Q (H&#39; a)) ∘ (g a)) ~ (g&#39; a)) (h : Σ B Q → T) →
      Id ( eq-htpy
           ( λ a → eq-htpy
             ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma H&#39; K (ev-pair h) a)))
         ( ap ev-pair
           ( htpy-precomp (htpy-map-Σ Q H&#39; g K) T h)))
    ( λ g g&#39; K h → {!ind-htpy g (λ g&#39; K&#39; → (h : Σ B Q → T) →
      Id ( eq-htpy
           ( λ a → eq-htpy
             ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma refl-htpy (λ a → htpy-eq (K&#39; a)) (ev-pair h) a)))
         ( ap ev-pair
           ( htpy-precomp (htpy-map-Σ Q refl-htpy g (λ a → htpy-eq (K&#39; a))) T h))) ? (λ a → eq-htpy (K a)) h!})
    H g g&#39; K
  
  
flattening-pushout&#39; :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  (f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  (l : Level) →
  pullback-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
flattening-pushout&#39; f g c P Q e l T =
  is-pullback-top-is-pullback-bottom-cube-is-equiv
    ( ( map-Π (λ x → precomp-Π (map-equiv (pr1 e x)) (λ q → T))) ∘
      ( precomp-Π (pr1 c) (λ x → (Q x) → T)))
    ( ( map-Π (λ x → precomp-Π (map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) x)) (λ q → T))) ∘
      ( precomp-Π (pr1 (pr2 c)) (λ x → (Q x) → T)))
    ( precomp-Π f (λ a → (pr1 P a) → T))
    ( ( map-Π (λ s → precomp (map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)) T)) ∘
      ( precomp-Π g (λ b → (pr1 (pr2 P) b) → T)))
    ( precomp (map-Σ Q (pr1 c) (λ a → map-equiv (pr1 e a))) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ Q (pr1 (pr2 c)) (λ b → map-equiv (pr1 (pr2 e) b))) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id)) T)
    ( precomp (map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s))) T)
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ev-pair
    ( htpy-precomp
      ( htpy-map-Σ Q
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → map-equiv (pr1 e (f s)))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s)))
      ( T))
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    refl-htpy
    ( λ h → eq-htpy (λ s → eq-htpy
      ( coherence-bottom-flattening-lemma
        ( pr2 (pr2 c))
        ( λ s → inv-htpy (pr2 (pr2 e) s))
        ( h)
        ( s))))
    {!!}
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    is-equiv-ev-pair
    {!!}

flattening-pushout :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l4}
  (f : S → A) (g : S → B) (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l5 f g)
  ( Q : X → UU l5)
  ( e : equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam f g c Q)) →
  (l : Level) →
  universal-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
flattening-pushout f g c P Q e l =
  universal-property-pushout-pullback-property-pushout l
    ( map-Σ (pr1 P) f (λ s → id))
    ( map-Σ (pr1 (pr2 P)) g (λ s → map-equiv (pr2 (pr2 P) s)))
    ( cocone-flattening-pushout f g c P Q e)
    ( flattening-pushout&#39; f g c P Q e l)
